(layout/base/nsCSSFrameConstructor.cpp)**: This is the entry point for the frame tree construction pipeline. The nsCSSFrameConstructor class is responsible for converting the DOM tree into a frame tree that mirrors the CSS display model. It constructs frames based on CSS display types and handles dynamic updates when content changes. The constructor maintains state about the frame tree and coordinates with the PresShell to schedule reflows when the tree structure changes.\\n\\n**Block Layout Reflow (layout/generic/)**: The block layout reflow mechanism is distributed across several key files:\\n\\n- **nsBlockFrame.cpp/h** implements the main reflow algorithm for block-level and block-equivalent frames. It uses BlockReflowState to manage state during reflow and handles line breaking, float management, and child frame layout.\\n\\n- **BlockReflowState.cpp/h** (initialized at BlockReflowState::BlockReflowState, line 31) maintains the state required for block reflow operations, including float positioning, available space management, and margin collapsing logic. It tracks the float manager state and provides methods like GetAvailableSpace() to determine layout constraints.\\n\\n- **nsBlockReflowContext.cpp/h** wraps the reflow of individual child frames within a block context. It handles the reflowing of child frames and computes their metrics relative to the containing block.\\n\\n**Inline Layout Reflow (layout/generic/)**: The inline layout pipeline is implemented through:\\n\\n- **nsLineLayout.cpp/h** (constructor at line 48) manages the reflowing of inline content within lines. It coordinates the layout of inline frames, text frames, and floats within a single line of text, including text wrapping and baseline alignment.\\n\\n- **nsLineBox.cpp/h** represents individual lines of content and maintains their state (clean/dirty flags), which is central to the invalidation mechanism.\\n\\n**Reflow Input/Output (layout/generic/)**:\\n\\n- **ReflowInput.cpp/h** (constructor at line 149) encapsulates all input information needed for a reflow operation, including available space, style information, containing block context, and parent reflow input. This is passed down the frame tree during reflow.\\n\\n- **ReflowOutput.cpp/h** carries the results of a reflow operation back up the tree, including size metrics and overflow information.\\n\\n**Dirty Frame Invalidation (layout/base/PresShell.cpp)**: This is the critical mechanism for tracking which frames need reflow:\\n\\n- **PresShell::FrameNeedsReflow()** (lines 2632-2680) is the central function that marks frames as dirty and enqueues them for reflow. Sets dirty state bits on the frame (NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY or NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN)\\n  2. Walks up the frame tree to find the next reflow root\\n  3. Triggers the refresh driver to schedule a reflow\\n\\n- The function handles different root handling modes and can mark either the frame itself or its descendants as dirty, controlling the scope of the subsequent reflow.\\n\\n**Base Frame Infrastructure (layout/generic/)**:\\n\\n- **nsIFrame.cpp/h** (Reflow method at line 7622) defines the base virtual Reflow() method that all frame types override.
